data-apiary-widget-id="/devToolsInit"></div><div data-apiary-widget-name="@marketplace/CartService" data-apiary-widget-id="/cartService"></div><div data-apiary-widget-name="@marketplace/FontLoader" data-apiary-widget-id="/fontLoader"></div><!--BEGIN [@marketplace/AnchorScroller] /anchorScroller static--><script nonce="">(function () {
  const MIN_SPEED = 0.1;
  const MAX_SPEED = 0.8;
  const HOST = location.host;
  const PATHNAME = unifyPath(location.pathname);
  const DURATION = 800; // [ms]

  function getLinkParent(element) {
    if (element === document.body) {
      return null;
    } else if (element.tagName === 'A') {
      return element;
    }

    return getLinkParent(element.parentNode);
  }

  function unifyPath(path) {
    return path.replace(/^\//, '');
  }

  function tick(speed, scrollY, scrollTargetY, currentTime = 0) {
    const _currentTime = currentTime + 1 / 60; //    


    const time = _currentTime / speed;
    const pos = getPosition(time);

    if (time < 1) {
      window.requestAnimationFrame(tick.bind(this, speed, scrollY, scrollTargetY, _currentTime));
      window.scrollTo(0, scrollY + (scrollTargetY - scrollY) * pos);
    } else {
      window.scrollTo(0, scrollTargetY);
    }
  }

  function getPosition(time) {
    return Math.sin(time * (Math.PI / 2));
  }

  function animateScroll(element) {
    const scrollY = window.scrollY;
    const scrollTargetY = window.pageYOffset + element.getBoundingClientRect().top;
    tick( //       ,       
    //   ( ,        
    //          )
    Math.max(MIN_SPEED, Math.min(Math.abs(scrollY - scrollTargetY) / DURATION, MAX_SPEED)), scrollY, scrollTargetY);
  }

  function onClick(event) {
    const link = getLinkParent(event.target);

    if (!link || !link.hash || link.host !== HOST || unifyPath(link.pathname) !== PATHNAME) {
      return;
    }

    const target = document.querySelector(link.hash) || document.querySelector(`[name=${link.hash.slice(1)}]`);

    if (!target) {
      return;
    }

    animateScroll(target);
    event.preventDefault();
  }

  window.document.body.addEventListener('click', onClick, true);
})();</script><!--END [@marketplace/AnchorScroller] /anchorScroller static--><div data-apiary-widget-name="@marketplace/PopupManager" data-apiary-widget-id="/popupManager"></div><div data-apiary-widget-name="@marketplace/AuthFink" data-apiary-widget-id="/authFink"><div class="" data-zone-data="{&quot;isLoggedIn&quot;:false,&quot;accountType&quot;:&quot;YANDEX&quot;}" data-zone-name="AuthFink"></div></div><div data-apiary-widget-name="@marketplace/AuthService" data-apiary-widget-id="/authService"></div><div data-apiary-widget-name="@marketplace/AuthProxyPopup" data-apiary-widget-id="/authProxyPopup"><div class="" data-zone-name="AuthProxyPopup" data-reactroot=""></div></div><div class="_3q8b-HlwVI" id="ROOT_DRAWER_ID" data-tid="8c732448"><div class="v8xIE9ivsy"><div><!--BEGIN [@yandex-market/mandrel/DevTools/Root] /devToolsRoot--><!--END [@yandex-market/mandrel/DevTools/Root] /devToolsRoot--></div></div></div><div></div></body></html>
